YES

********************************************************************************
Proof Outline:

Remains to prove termination of a 24-rules system (24 strict rules).
Applying sparse untiling TRFCU(2) after reversal [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 16-rules system (16 strict rules).
Removing 1 rule by a matrix interpretation of dimension 4 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 15-rules system (15 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TRFC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 688-rules system (688 strict rules).
Removing 12 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 676-rules system (676 strict rules).
Removing 14 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 662-rules system (662 strict rules).
Removing 20 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 642-rules system (642 strict rules).
Applying sparse untiling TRFCU(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 109-rules system (109 strict rules).
Removing 92 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 17-rules system (17 strict rules).
Removing 10 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 7-rules system (7 strict rules).
Removing 7 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 0-rules system (0 strict rules).
QED
